<s> the decoration was really in excellent taste <\s>

<s> he admired extremely the purple leather curtains drawn along one entire side framing a huge white tiled stove <\s>
<s> the central partitions of the skylight had been slid back and the warm air from outside penetrated into the very heart of the house <\s>

<s> after writing to bosinney in the terms that have already been chronicled soames had dismissed the cost of the house from his mind <\s>
<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>
<s> the attitude of the confident and friendly husband was gone <\s>
<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>

<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>

<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>

<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>

<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>

<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>

<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>
<s> the attitude of the confident and friendly husband was gone <\s>
<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>
<s> he had said to bosinney when he could speak and i suppose you're perfectly contented with yourself <\s>
<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>
<s> what he meant by those words he did not quite know at the time but after dinner he looked up the correspondence between himself and bosinney to make quite sure <\s>
<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>
<s> he was looking at his wife's face when he came to this conclusion <\s>
<s> seated in her usual seat on the sofa she was altering the lace on a collar <\s>
<s> she had not once spoken to him all the evening <\s>
<s> he went up to the mantelpiece and contemplating his face in the mirror said your friend the buccaneer has made a fool of himself he will have to pay for it <\s>
<s> she looked at him scornfully and answered i don't know what you are talking about <\s>
<s> a mere trifle quite beneath your contempt four hundred pounds <\s>
<s> do you mean that you are going to make him pay that towards this hateful house <\s>
<s> and you know he's got nothing <\s>
<s> then you are meaner than i thought you <\s>
<s> soames turned from the mirror and unconsciously taking a china cup from the mantelpiece clasped his hands around it as though praying <\s>
<s> he saw her bosom rise and fall her eyes darkening with anger and taking no notice of the taunt he asked quietly are you carrying on a flirtation with bosinney <\s>
<s> no i am not <\s>
<s> her eyes met his and he looked away <\s>
<s> he neither believed nor disbelieved her but he knew that he had made a mistake in asking he never had known never would know what she was thinking <\s>
<s> the sight of her inscrutable face the thought of all the hundreds of evenings he had seen her sitting there like that soft and passive but unreadable unknown enraged him beyond measure <\s>
<s> i believe you are made of stone he said clenching his fingers so hard that he broke the fragile cup <\s>
<s> the pieces fell into the grate <\s>
<s> you seem to forget she said that cup is not <\s>
<s> soames gripped her arm <\s>
<s> a good beating he said is the only thing that would bring you to your senses but turning on his heel he left the room <\s>
<s> chapter xiv soames sits on the stairs soames went up stairs that night with the feeling that he had gone too far <\s>
<s> he was prepared to offer excuses for his words <\s>
<s> he turned out the gas still burning in the passage outside their room <\s>
<s> pausing with his hand on the knob of the door he tried to shape his apology for he had no intention of letting her see that he was nervous <\s>
<s> but the door did not open nor when he pulled it and turned the handle firmly <\s>
<s> she must have locked it for some reason and forgotten <\s>
<s> entering his dressing room where the gas was also lighted and burning low he went quickly to the other door <\s>
<s> that too was locked <\s>
<s> then he noticed that the camp bed which he occasionally used was prepared and his sleeping suit laid out upon it <\s>
<s> he put his hand up to his forehead and brought it away wet <\s>
<s> it dawned on him that he was barred out <\s>
<s> he went back to the door and rattling the handle stealthily called unlock the door do you hear <\s>
<s> there was a faint rustling but no answer <\s>
<s> james did not know what on earth to answer <\s>
<s> the bright hot morning had changed slowly to a grey oppressive afternoon a heavy bank of clouds with the yellow tinge of coming thunder had risen in the south and was creeping up <\s>
<s> the branches of the trees dropped motionless across the road without the smallest stir of foliage <\s>
<s> a faint odour of glue from the heated horses clung in the thick air the coachman and groom rigid and unbending exchanged stealthy murmurs on the box without ever turning their heads <\s>
<s> to james great relief they reached the house at last the silence and impenetrability of this woman by his side whom he had always thought so soft and mild alarmed him <\s>
<s> the carriage put them down at the door and they entered <\s>
<s> the hall was cool and so still that it was like passing into a tomb a shudder ran down james's spine <\s>
<s> he quickly lifted the heavy leather curtains between the columns into the inner court <\s>
<s> he could not restrain an exclamation of approval <\s>
<s> the decoration was really in excellent taste <\s>
<s> the dull ruby tiles that extended from the foot of the walls to the verge of a circular clump of tall iris plants surrounding in turn a sunken basin of white marble filled with water were obviously of the best quality <\s>
<s> he admired extremely the purple leather curtains drawn along one entire side framing a huge white tiled stove <\s>
<s> the central partitions of the skylight had been slid back and the warm air from outside penetrated into the very heart of the house <\s>
<s> he stood his hands behind him his head bent back on his high narrow shoulders spying the tracery on the columns and the pattern of the frieze which ran round the ivory coloured walls under the gallery <\s>
<s> evidently no pains had been spared <\s>
<s> it was quite the house of a gentleman <\s>
<s> he went up to the curtains and having discovered how they were worked drew them asunder and disclosed the picture gallery ending in a great window taking up the whole end of the room <\s>
<s> it had a black oak floor and its walls again were of ivory white <\s>
<s> he went on throwing open doors and peeping in <\s>
<s> everything was in apple pie order ready for immediate occupation <\s>
<s> he turned round at last to speak to irene and saw her standing over in the garden entrance with her husband and bosinney <\s>
<s> though not remarkable for sensibility james felt at once that something was wrong <\s>
<s> he went up to them and vaguely alarmed ignorant of the nature of the trouble made an attempt to smooth things over <\s>
<s> how are you mr <\s>
<s> he said holding out his hand <\s>
<s> you've been spending money pretty freely down here i should say <\s>
<s> soames turned his back and walked away <\s>

<s> so much the worse for him this time <\s>

<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>
<s> he had said to bosinney when he could speak and i suppose you're perfectly contented with yourself <\s>
<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>
<s> what he meant by those words he did not quite know at the time but after dinner he looked up the correspondence between himself and bosinney to make quite sure <\s>
<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>
<s> he was looking at his wife's face when he came to this conclusion <\s>
<s> seated in her usual seat on the sofa she was altering the lace on a collar <\s>
<s> she had not once spoken to him all the evening <\s>
<s> he went up to the mantelpiece and contemplating his face in the mirror said your friend the buccaneer has made a fool of himself he will have to pay for it <\s>
<s> she looked at him scornfully and answered i don't know what you are talking about <\s>
<s> a mere trifle quite beneath your contempt four hundred pounds <\s>
<s> do you mean that you are going to make him pay that towards this hateful house <\s>
<s> and you know he's got nothing <\s>
<s> then you are meaner than i thought you <\s>

<s> he saw her bosom rise and fall her eyes darkening with anger and taking no notice of the taunt he asked quietly are you carrying on a flirtation with bosinney <\s>
<s> no i am not <\s>
<s> her eyes met his and he looked away <\s>
<s> he neither believed nor disbelieved her but he knew that he had made a mistake in asking he never had known never would know what she was thinking <\s>
<s> the sight of her inscrutable face the thought of all the hundreds of evenings he had seen her sitting there like that soft and passive but unreadable unknown enraged him beyond measure <\s>

<s> a good beating he said is the only thing that would bring you to your senses but turning on his heel he left the room <\s>

<s> the bright hot morning had changed slowly to a grey oppressive afternoon a heavy bank of clouds with the yellow tinge of coming thunder had risen in the south and was creeping up <\s>
<s> the branches of the trees dropped motionless across the road without the smallest stir of foliage <\s>

<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>

<s> the decoration was really in excellent taste <\s>

<s> he admired extremely the purple leather curtains drawn along one entire side framing a huge white tiled stove <\s>
<s> the central partitions of the skylight had been slid back and the warm air from outside penetrated into the very heart of the house <\s>

<s> after writing to bosinney in the terms that have already been chronicled soames had dismissed the cost of the house from his mind <\s>
<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>
<s> the attitude of the confident and friendly husband was gone <\s>
<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>

<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>

<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>

<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>

<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>

<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>

<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>
<s> the attitude of the confident and friendly husband was gone <\s>
<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>
<s> he had said to bosinney when he could speak and i suppose you're perfectly contented with yourself <\s>
<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>
<s> what he meant by those words he did not quite know at the time but after dinner he looked up the correspondence between himself and bosinney to make quite sure <\s>
<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>
<s> he was looking at his wife's face when he came to this conclusion <\s>
<s> seated in her usual seat on the sofa she was altering the lace on a collar <\s>
<s> she had not once spoken to him all the evening <\s>
<s> he went up to the mantelpiece and contemplating his face in the mirror said your friend the buccaneer has made a fool of himself he will have to pay for it <\s>
<s> she looked at him scornfully and answered i don't know what you are talking about <\s>
<s> a mere trifle quite beneath your contempt four hundred pounds <\s>
<s> do you mean that you are going to make him pay that towards this hateful house <\s>
<s> and you know he's got nothing <\s>
<s> then you are meaner than i thought you <\s>
<s> soames turned from the mirror and unconsciously taking a china cup from the mantelpiece clasped his hands around it as though praying <\s>
<s> he saw her bosom rise and fall her eyes darkening with anger and taking no notice of the taunt he asked quietly are you carrying on a flirtation with bosinney <\s>
<s> no i am not <\s>
<s> her eyes met his and he looked away <\s>
<s> he neither believed nor disbelieved her but he knew that he had made a mistake in asking he never had known never would know what she was thinking <\s>
<s> the sight of her inscrutable face the thought of all the hundreds of evenings he had seen her sitting there like that soft and passive but unreadable unknown enraged him beyond measure <\s>
<s> i believe you are made of stone he said clenching his fingers so hard that he broke the fragile cup <\s>
<s> the pieces fell into the grate <\s>
<s> you seem to forget she said that cup is not <\s>
<s> soames gripped her arm <\s>
<s> a good beating he said is the only thing that would bring you to your senses but turning on his heel he left the room <\s>
<s> chapter xiv soames sits on the stairs soames went up stairs that night with the feeling that he had gone too far <\s>
<s> he was prepared to offer excuses for his words <\s>
<s> he turned out the gas still burning in the passage outside their room <\s>
<s> pausing with his hand on the knob of the door he tried to shape his apology for he had no intention of letting her see that he was nervous <\s>
<s> but the door did not open nor when he pulled it and turned the handle firmly <\s>
<s> she must have locked it for some reason and forgotten <\s>
<s> entering his dressing room where the gas was also lighted and burning low he went quickly to the other door <\s>
<s> that too was locked <\s>
<s> then he noticed that the camp bed which he occasionally used was prepared and his sleeping suit laid out upon it <\s>
<s> he put his hand up to his forehead and brought it away wet <\s>
<s> it dawned on him that he was barred out <\s>
<s> he went back to the door and rattling the handle stealthily called unlock the door do you hear <\s>
<s> there was a faint rustling but no answer <\s>
<s> james did not know what on earth to answer <\s>
<s> the bright hot morning had changed slowly to a grey oppressive afternoon a heavy bank of clouds with the yellow tinge of coming thunder had risen in the south and was creeping up <\s>
<s> the branches of the trees dropped motionless across the road without the smallest stir of foliage <\s>
<s> a faint odour of glue from the heated horses clung in the thick air the coachman and groom rigid and unbending exchanged stealthy murmurs on the box without ever turning their heads <\s>
<s> to james great relief they reached the house at last the silence and impenetrability of this woman by his side whom he had always thought so soft and mild alarmed him <\s>
<s> the carriage put them down at the door and they entered <\s>
<s> the hall was cool and so still that it was like passing into a tomb a shudder ran down james's spine <\s>
<s> he quickly lifted the heavy leather curtains between the columns into the inner court <\s>
<s> he could not restrain an exclamation of approval <\s>
<s> the decoration was really in excellent taste <\s>
<s> the dull ruby tiles that extended from the foot of the walls to the verge of a circular clump of tall iris plants surrounding in turn a sunken basin of white marble filled with water were obviously of the best quality <\s>
<s> he admired extremely the purple leather curtains drawn along one entire side framing a huge white tiled stove <\s>
<s> the central partitions of the skylight had been slid back and the warm air from outside penetrated into the very heart of the house <\s>
<s> he stood his hands behind him his head bent back on his high narrow shoulders spying the tracery on the columns and the pattern of the frieze which ran round the ivory coloured walls under the gallery <\s>
<s> evidently no pains had been spared <\s>
<s> it was quite the house of a gentleman <\s>
<s> he went up to the curtains and having discovered how they were worked drew them asunder and disclosed the picture gallery ending in a great window taking up the whole end of the room <\s>
<s> it had a black oak floor and its walls again were of ivory white <\s>
<s> he went on throwing open doors and peeping in <\s>
<s> everything was in apple pie order ready for immediate occupation <\s>
<s> he turned round at last to speak to irene and saw her standing over in the garden entrance with her husband and bosinney <\s>
<s> though not remarkable for sensibility james felt at once that something was wrong <\s>
<s> he went up to them and vaguely alarmed ignorant of the nature of the trouble made an attempt to smooth things over <\s>
<s> how are you mr <\s>
<s> he said holding out his hand <\s>
<s> you've been spending money pretty freely down here i should say <\s>
<s> soames turned his back and walked away <\s>

<s> so much the worse for him this time <\s>

<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>
<s> he had said to bosinney when he could speak and i suppose you're perfectly contented with yourself <\s>
<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>
<s> what he meant by those words he did not quite know at the time but after dinner he looked up the correspondence between himself and bosinney to make quite sure <\s>
<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>
<s> he was looking at his wife's face when he came to this conclusion <\s>
<s> seated in her usual seat on the sofa she was altering the lace on a collar <\s>
<s> she had not once spoken to him all the evening <\s>
<s> he went up to the mantelpiece and contemplating his face in the mirror said your friend the buccaneer has made a fool of himself he will have to pay for it <\s>
<s> she looked at him scornfully and answered i don't know what you are talking about <\s>
<s> a mere trifle quite beneath your contempt four hundred pounds <\s>
<s> do you mean that you are going to make him pay that towards this hateful house <\s>
<s> and you know he's got nothing <\s>
<s> then you are meaner than i thought you <\s>

<s> he saw her bosom rise and fall her eyes darkening with anger and taking no notice of the taunt he asked quietly are you carrying on a flirtation with bosinney <\s>
<s> no i am not <\s>
<s> her eyes met his and he looked away <\s>
<s> he neither believed nor disbelieved her but he knew that he had made a mistake in asking he never had known never would know what she was thinking <\s>
<s> the sight of her inscrutable face the thought of all the hundreds of evenings he had seen her sitting there like that soft and passive but unreadable unknown enraged him beyond measure <\s>

<s> a good beating he said is the only thing that would bring you to your senses but turning on his heel he left the room <\s>

<s> the bright hot morning had changed slowly to a grey oppressive afternoon a heavy bank of clouds with the yellow tinge of coming thunder had risen in the south and was creeping up <\s>
<s> the branches of the trees dropped motionless across the road without the smallest stir of foliage <\s>

<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>

<s> the branches of the trees dropped motionless across the road without the smallest stir of foliage <\s>
<s> a faint odour of glue from the heated horses clung in the thick air the coachman and groom rigid and unbending exchanged stealthy murmurs on the box without ever turning their heads <\s>
<s> to james great relief they reached the house at last the silence and impenetrability of this woman by his side whom he had always thought so soft and mild alarmed him <\s>
<s> the carriage put them down at the door and they entered <\s>
<s> the hall was cool and so still that it was like passing into a tomb a shudder ran down james's spine <\s>

<s> he could not restrain an exclamation of approval <\s>
<s> the decoration was really in excellent taste <\s>
<s> the dull ruby tiles that extended from the foot of the walls to the verge of a circular clump of tall iris plants surrounding in turn a sunken basin of white marble filled with water were obviously of the best quality <\s>
<s> he admired extremely the purple leather curtains drawn along one entire side framing a huge white tiled stove <\s>
<s> the central partitions of the skylight had been slid back and the warm air from outside penetrated into the very heart of the house <\s>
<s> he stood his hands behind him his head bent back on his high narrow shoulders spying the tracery on the columns and the pattern of the frieze which ran round the ivory coloured walls under the gallery <\s>
<s> evidently no pains had been spared <\s>
<s> it was quite the house of a gentleman <\s>
<s> he went up to the curtains and having discovered how they were worked drew them asunder and disclosed the picture gallery ending in a great window taking up the whole end of the room <\s>
<s> it had a black oak floor and its walls again were of ivory white <\s>
<s> he went on throwing open doors and peeping in <\s>
<s> everything was in apple pie order ready for immediate occupation <\s>
<s> he turned round at last to speak to irene and saw her standing over in the garden entrance with her husband and bosinney <\s>
<s> though not remarkable for sensibility james felt at once that something was wrong <\s>

<s> nothing in this world is more sure to upset a forsyte than the discovery that something on which he has stipulated to spend a certain sum has cost more <\s>
<s> and this is reasonable for upon the accuracy of his estimates the whole policy of his life is ordered <\s>
<s> if he cannot rely on definite values of property his compass is amiss he is adrift upon bitter waters without a helm <\s>
<s> after writing to bosinney in the terms that have already been chronicled soames had dismissed the cost of the house from his mind <\s>
<s> he believed that he had made the matter of the final cost so very plain that the possibility of its being again exceeded had really never entered his head <\s>
<s> on hearing from bosinney that his limit of twelve thousand pounds would be exceeded by something like four hundred he had grown white with anger <\s>
<s> his original estimate of the cost of the house completed had been ten thousand pounds and he had often blamed himself severely for allowing himself to be led into repeated excesses <\s>
<s> over this last expenditure however bosinney had put himself completely in the wrong <\s>
<s> how on earth a fellow could make such an ass of himself soames could not conceive but he had done so and all the rancour and hidden jealousy that had been burning against him for so long was now focussed in rage at this crowning piece of extravagance <\s>
<s> the attitude of the confident and friendly husband was gone <\s>
<s> to preserve property his wife he had assumed it to preserve property of another kind he lost it now <\s>
<s> he had said to bosinney when he could speak and i suppose you're perfectly contented with yourself <\s>
<s> but i may as well tell you that you've altogether mistaken your man <\s>
<s> what he meant by those words he did not quite know at the time but after dinner he looked up the correspondence between himself and bosinney to make quite sure <\s>
<s> there could be no two opinions about it the fellow had made himself liable for that extra four hundred or at all events for three hundred and fifty of it and he would have to make it good <\s>
<s> he was looking at his wife's face when he came to this conclusion <\s>
<s> seated in her usual seat on the sofa she was altering the lace on a collar <\s>
<s> she had not once spoken to him all the evening <\s>
<s> he went up to the mantelpiece and contemplating his face in the mirror said your friend the buccaneer has made a fool of himself he will have to pay for it <\s>
<s> she looked at him scornfully and answered i don't know what you are talking about <\s>
<s> a mere trifle quite beneath your contempt four hundred pounds <\s>
<s> do you mean that you are going to make him pay that towards this hateful house <\s>
<s> and you know he's got nothing <\s>
<s> then you are meaner than i thought you <\s>

<s> no i am not <\s>
<s> her eyes met his and he looked away <\s>
<s> he neither believed nor disbelieved her but he knew that he had made a mistake in asking he never had known never would know what she was thinking <\s>
